(function () {
    var findAbNames = function() {
        var cookies=document.cookie.split(';');
        var c,s,t;
        for ( var asdf = 0 ; asdf < cookies.length ; asdf++ ) {
            c = cookies[asdf].trim();
            if ( 0 === c.indexOf('ab_name_') ) {
                s = c.split('=');
                if ( 2 === s.length ) {

                    if ( undefined === HDN.abData[s[0].substr(8)] ) {
                        HDN.abData[s[0].substr(8)] = ( 'A' === s[1] ? 'C' : 'V1' );
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    };

        delete(HDN.abData['_hasData']);

            window.aps.abtest += ',';
        }
        window.aps.abtest += abDataTmp.join(',');
    }

      <script>
       function initSailthru() {
	var injectAsyncScript = function (url, callback) {
		var iscript = document.createElement("script");
		iscript.type = "text/javascript";
		iscript.async = true;
		iscript.src = url;
		if (typeof callback === "function") {
		iscript.onload = iscript.onreadystatechange = function () {
			if (!this.readyState || this.readyState === "loaded" || this.readyState === "complete") {
				try {
					callback();
				} catch (err) { }
			}
		};
		} (document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0] || document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0]).appendChild(iscript);
	};

	injectAsyncScript("https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery-validate/1.16.0/jquery.validate.min.js", function () {
		$('form[data-sailthru-nl-list-id]').each(function () {
			$(this).validate({
				errorPlacement: function (error) {
          $('.st-nl-error-message').html(error.text());
				}, 
				rules: { userEmail: { required: true, email: true } }, 
				messages: { userEmail: "Please enter a valid email address." }, 
				submitHandler: function (form, evt) {
					evt.preventDefault();
					var userEmail, lists, urlParams, source;

					form = $(form);
					userEmail = form.find('[name="userEmail"]').val();
					lists = { "SFC_NL_TopStories": 1 };
					urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
					source = urlParams.has('gclid') ? form.attr("data-sailthru-nl-source") + "_GAW" : form.attr("data-sailthru-nl-source");
					
					Sailthru.integration("userSignUp", {
						"email": userEmail, 
            "lists": lists, 
            "source": source, 
            "onSuccess": function () {
							form.find(".st-nl-input").hide();
							form.find(".st-nl-error-message").hide();
							form.find(".st-nl-submit-message").html("Thank you for signing up!");
							Sailthru.integration("customEvent", { "name": "optin_user", "email": userEmail });
						}, 
            "onError": function () {
							form.find(".st-nl-error-message").html("We encountered an issue signing you up. Please try again").fadeOut(5000);
							form.find(".st-nl-input").delay(4500).fadeIn(5000);
						}
					});
				}
			});
		});
	});

	injectAsyncScript("https://ak.sail-horizon.com/spm/spm.v1.min.js", function () {
		Sailthru.init({ "customerId": "fca2a0390286f0e53120a668534d9529" });
	});

	bcTrackData('impression','Inline Subscription Unit','view','PHD Inline Subscription Marketing Unit May 2019');
} 

if (document.readyState === "complete" || (document.readyState !== "loading" && !document.documentElement.doScroll)) {
	initSailthru();
} else {
	document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
		initSailthru();
	});
}
      </script>
     </div>

      <script>
       $.get( "https://files.sfchronicle.com/project-feeds/leah_garchik_eavesdropping_live_quotes.json", function( data ) {
    var d = new Date();
    var n = d.getDay();
    let chosen = data[0];
    try {
      if (data[n-1]){
        chosen = data[n-1];
      }
    } catch (err) {
      chosen = data[0];
    }
    $("#garchik-quote").html(chosen.quote);
    $("#garchik-source").text(chosen.source);
    $("#garchik-contrib").text(chosen.contributor);
    $(".content-container").show();
  });
      </script>
